They covered all ages. Great park!
1-10 years old - playground,
Teenager's/adults - skate area, basketball, football field, small and big tennis area
Senior's - walking path, exercise area.
Sitting area for lunch with bbq coil areas. Excellent. Just one thing, need more shade for summer, more trees or artificial umbrellas.< /text>

<Name>Steve Brown< /Name>< date>
1581994541292</date>
<rating>5</rating>< Review>
This is a great park for what it's worth to me. I'm only visiting but it's my go to park. There's a lot of amenities/activities-Goleta Skatepark,jungle gym,small basketball courts for little hoopsters,1 full size courts for us,table tennis,chess and a field large enough for soccer. I almost forgot that there's a paved walkway for a small nature trail. I haven't been on it or know where it goes but it still looks pretty cool and it's  wheelchair accessible. The only drawback to me is the lack of parking,but it's still a great park. I almost forgot that the unisex restroom/changing rooms were awesome too! Very clean & safe and equipped with soap & the coolest hand dryer I've seen in a public place.  The Dyson blade is great for drying off. Santa Barbara great job & kudos to the park staff and the upkeep of a great neighborhood facility. Good job everyone.</Review>

< text>
Businesses are about generating money to enrich themselves by any mean possible. LAHSA may have "homeless services" as part of the name, but in truth they are JUST ANOTHER BUSINESS.

Homelessness businesses are not required to be publicly transparent with their policies, so they need never worry about being held accountable for any transgressions. <Time>1584754234404<//Time>< Review>
I'm grateful they are so kind, do good business and have a nice, clean place and good prices. Really nice people run this location, very approachable and pleasant. Angel and Daniel have run this location for years and surprise me when they know me by name outside of the office. Prices are good but insurance is no longer optional, it's included (almost gave 4 stars since it's not optional). Office hours are good. Gate hours are awesome, closing at 10:30pm. There's a lot of locker options, indoor lockers with typical room doors and larger spaces are outdoor with roll top doors. Rental parking spaces available for small vehicles upto full size RVs. Carts for moving your stuff are available. Pretty clean and nice looking place. Bathrooms aren't always unlocked due to other renters ruining it for us but they have restrooms unlike a lot of places, just ask someone for help. Cameras are watching almost everywhere too. I even noticed a pest control pouch slid under door one day so they are on top of that too. Overall, definitely where you want to go for self storage.< /Review>

< review>
I called around each and every storage facility in the Santa Maria-Nipomo area down to the buellton-solvang area and the best deal I found was here at extra space storage. The price combined with the hours I can access my unit open until 10pm (on farnel Rd. by blosser Walmart). Not only was I greeted with professionalism and courtesy I was given a better deal than they quoted me over the phone just hours before. When I arrived, the place was well kept- neat and orderly. It was reassuring that the manager lives on site and frequently patrols the area while quickly addressing unfamiliar people or ones who strayed too far from their own unit with a friendly reminder that he's watching. They have plenty of options as far as indoor or outdoor availability on to storing your furnishings from an entire 3 bedroom house (R.V. and car too) or just enough space for  your mini fridge and toaster. Angel and Daniel run a tight ship here and are very competitive with their pricing. I highly recommend storing here, or at least taking the walk through to see for yourself. I've been here for almost 3 years with no issues whatsoever.</review>

Great service from Angel. He was very helpful and accommodating. I really like that this eco-friendly company has gone paperless as well. The location is easy to find and very well maintained.

The storage unit complex where my unit was located is not climate-controlled so it was very hot and stuffy, but that's not a dealbreaker. <userid>113253025460230544097</userid>< text>
My Frigidaire Gallery Stove tops gas valve broke.  This caused the top left burner to not turn off, to turn it off I had to turn the gas valve off.  I call Oak Valley, they were on time and communicated and even gave me a 15 min heads up call.

Jeremy and Scott were professional, courteous and wore a mask the entire time they were in our home.  He explained to me that the valve was broken and needed to be replaced.  He spent 15 mins researching the part and told me it was on back order, no ETA would be given.  And that the part might be end of life.  He gave me the part number, I researched it and no one had it.  Since the stove top is 10 years old  the manufacture isn't required to make parts anymore.

With knowing this I ordered a new stove top, after 3 weeks of the initial consultation I purchased a new stove top from Lowes.  I received a call a day later from Oak Valley, telling me that they received the part.

They were able to fix my stove top and save me $2k.  My range is back to working order, and I couldn't be happier.  I without hesitation recommend them for any repairs.< /text>
